**GT expression (simplified):**

```
= -1.1994*epsilon*T + 419.87*epsilon + 5.2295*T*epsilon^0.9585 - 1726.1*epsilon^0.9585
```

So GT has the form:
```
a*epsilon*T + b*epsilon + c*T*epsilon^p + d*epsilon^p
```
where p ≈ 0.9585.

This can be rewritten as:
```
epsilon*T*(a) + epsilon*(b) + epsilon^p*T*(c) + epsilon^p*(d)
```

Or equivalently:
```
T*(a*epsilon + c*epsilon^p) + (b*epsilon + d*epsilon^p)
```

The key basis functions are: `epsilon*T`, `epsilon`, `T*epsilon^p`, `epsilon^p` where p ≈ 0.9585.

Now let me check each candidate for structural compatibility. The GT depends **linearly on T**, so candidates must have terms linear in T (not sqrt(T), T^2, etc.) unless they can be made equivalent.

**Critical observation:** Most candidates use `sqrt(T)` as their T-dependence. The GT requires terms linear in T. Since `sqrt(T)` and `T` are linearly independent functions, `sqrt(T)` cannot match `T` for all T values. This eliminates many candidates immediately.

**Candidate 45:** `T*c0*epsilon^c1 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*exp(c5*epsilon) + c6*sin(c7*log(c8*epsilon+1)+c9)`
Only one T-dependent term. Cannot match.
